173class WBIsKlassAliveClosure : public LockedClassesDo {
174 Symbol* _name;
175 int _count;
176public:
177 WBIsKlassAliveClosure(Symbol* name) : _name(name), _count(0) {}
178
179 void do_klass(Klass* k) {
180 Symbol* ksym = k->name();
181 if (ksym->fast_compare(_name) == 0) {
182 _count++;
183 } else if (k->is_instance_klass()) {
184 // Need special handling for hidden classes because the JVM
185 // appends "+<hex-address>" to hidden class names.
186 InstanceKlass *ik = InstanceKlass::cast(k);
187 if (ik->is_hidden()) {
188 ResourceMark rm;
189 char* k_name = ksym->as_C_string();
190 // Find the first '+' char and truncate the string at that point.
191 // NOTE: This will not work correctly if the original hidden class
192 // name contains a '+'.
193 char* plus_char = strchr(k_name, '+');
194 if (plus_char != NULL__null) {
195 *plus_char = 0;
196 char* c_name = _name->as_C_string();
197 if (strcmp(c_name, k_name) == 0) {
198 _count++;
199 }
200 }
201 }
202 }
203 }
204
205 int count() const {
206 return _count;
207 }
208};

210WB_ENTRY(jint, WB_CountAliveClasses(JNIEnv* env, jobject target, jstring name))extern "C" { jint WB_CountAliveClasses(JNIEnv* env, jobject target
, jstring name) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current
()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 210, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
211 oop h_name = JNIHandles::resolve(name);
212 if (h_name == NULL__null) return false;
213 Symbol* sym = java_lang_String::as_symbol(h_name);
214 TempNewSymbol tsym(sym); // Make sure to decrement reference count on sym on return
215
216 WBIsKlassAliveClosure closure(sym);
217 ClassLoaderDataGraph::classes_do(&closure);
218
219 // Return the count of alive classes with this name.
220 return closure.count();
221WB_END} }

271WB_ENTRY(void, WB_ReadFromNoaccessArea(JNIEnv* env, jobject o))extern "C" { void WB_ReadFromNoaccessArea(JNIEnv* env, jobject
o) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current
()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 271, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
272 size_t granularity = os::vm_allocation_granularity();
273 ReservedHeapSpace rhs(100 * granularity, granularity, os::vm_page_size());
274 VirtualSpace vs;
275 vs.initialize(rhs, 50 * granularity);
276
277 // Check if constraints are complied
278 if (!( UseCompressedOops && rhs.base() != NULL__null &&
279 CompressedOops::base() != NULL__null &&
280 CompressedOops::use_implicit_null_checks() )) {
281 tty->print_cr("WB_ReadFromNoaccessArea method is useless:\n "
282 "\tUseCompressedOops is %d\n"
283 "\trhs.base() is " PTR_FORMAT"0x%016" "l" "x" "\n"
284 "\tCompressedOops::base() is " PTR_FORMAT"0x%016" "l" "x" "\n"
285 "\tCompressedOops::use_implicit_null_checks() is %d",
286 UseCompressedOops,
287 p2i(rhs.base()),
288 p2i(CompressedOops::base()),
289 CompressedOops::use_implicit_null_checks());
290 return;
291 }
292 tty->print_cr("Reading from no access area... ");
293 tty->print_cr("*(vs.low_boundary() - rhs.noaccess_prefix() / 2 ) = %c",
294 *(vs.low_boundary() - rhs.noaccess_prefix() / 2 ));
295WB_END} }
296
297static jint wb_stress_virtual_space_resize(size_t reserved_space_size,
298 size_t magnitude, size_t iterations) {
299 size_t granularity = os::vm_allocation_granularity();
300 ReservedHeapSpace rhs(reserved_space_size * granularity, granularity, os::vm_page_size());
301 VirtualSpace vs;
302 if (!vs.initialize(rhs, 0)) {
303 tty->print_cr("Failed to initialize VirtualSpace. Can't proceed.");
304 return 3;
305 }
306
307 int seed = os::random();
308 tty->print_cr("Random seed is %d", seed);
309
310 for (size_t i = 0; i < iterations; i++) {
311
312 // Whether we will shrink or grow
313 bool shrink = os::random() % 2L == 0;
314
315 // Get random delta to resize virtual space
316 size_t delta = (size_t)os::random() % magnitude;
317
318 // If we are about to shrink virtual space below zero, then expand instead
319 if (shrink && vs.committed_size() < delta) {
320 shrink = false;
321 }
322
323 // Resizing by delta
324 if (shrink) {
325 vs.shrink_by(delta);
326 } else {
327 // If expanding fails expand_by will silently return false
328 vs.expand_by(delta, true);
329 }
330 }
331 return 0;
332}
333
334WB_ENTRY(jint, WB_StressVirtualSpaceResize(JNIEnv* env, jobject o,extern "C" { jint WB_StressVirtualSpaceResize(JNIEnv* env, jobject
o, jlong reserved_space_size, jlong magnitude, jlong iterations
) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current
()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 335, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
335 jlong reserved_space_size, jlong magnitude, jlong iterations))extern "C" { jint WB_StressVirtualSpaceResize(JNIEnv* env, jobject
o, jlong reserved_space_size, jlong magnitude, jlong iterations
) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current
()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 335, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
336 tty->print_cr("reservedSpaceSize=" JLONG_FORMAT"%" "l" "d" ", magnitude=" JLONG_FORMAT"%" "l" "d" ", "
337 "iterations=" JLONG_FORMAT"%" "l" "d" "\n", reserved_space_size, magnitude,
338 iterations);
339 if (reserved_space_size < 0 || magnitude < 0 || iterations < 0) {
340 tty->print_cr("One of variables printed above is negative. Can't proceed.\n");
341 return 1;
342 }
343
344 // sizeof(size_t) depends on whether OS is 32bit or 64bit. sizeof(jlong) is
345 // always 8 byte. That's why we should avoid overflow in case of 32bit platform.
346 if (sizeof(size_t) < sizeof(jlong)) {
347 jlong size_t_max_value = (jlong) SIZE_T_MAX_VALUE((size_t) -1);
348 if (reserved_space_size > size_t_max_value || magnitude > size_t_max_value
349 || iterations > size_t_max_value) {
350 tty->print_cr("One of variables printed above overflows size_t. Can't proceed.\n");
351 return 2;
352 }
353 }
354
355 return wb_stress_virtual_space_resize((size_t) reserved_space_size,
356 (size_t) magnitude, (size_t) iterations);
357WB_END} }

o, jobject obj) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current
()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"

586
587class OldRegionsLivenessClosure: public HeapRegionClosure {
588
589 private:
590 const int _liveness;
591 size_t _total_count;
592 size_t _total_memory;
593 size_t _total_memory_to_free;
594
595 public:
596 OldRegionsLivenessClosure(int liveness) :
597 _liveness(liveness),
598 _total_count(0),
599 _total_memory(0),
600 _total_memory_to_free(0) { }
601
602 size_t total_count() { return _total_count; }
603 size_t total_memory() { return _total_memory; }
604 size_t total_memory_to_free() { return _total_memory_to_free; }
605
606 bool do_heap_region(HeapRegion* r) {
607 if (r->is_old()) {
608 size_t prev_live = r->marked_bytes();
609 size_t live = r->live_bytes();
610 size_t size = r->used();
611 size_t reg_size = HeapRegion::GrainBytes;
612 if (size > 0 && ((int)(live * 100 / size) < _liveness)) {
613 _total_memory += size;
614 ++_total_count;
615 if (size == reg_size) {
616 // we don't include non-full regions since they are unlikely included in mixed gc
617 // for testing purposes it's enough to have lowest estimation of total memory that is expected to be freed
618 _total_memory_to_free += size - prev_live;
619 }
620 }
621 }
622 return false;
623 }
624};
625
626
627WB_ENTRY(jlongArray, WB_G1GetMixedGCInfo(JNIEnv* env, jobject o, jint liveness))extern "C" { jlongArray WB_G1GetMixedGCInfo(JNIEnv* env, jobject
o, jint liveness) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current
()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 627, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
628 if (!UseG1GC) {
629 THROW_MSG_NULL(vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedOperationException(), "WB_G1GetMixedGCInfo: G1 GC is not enabled"){ Exceptions::_throw_msg(__the_thread__, "/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 629, vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedOperationException(), "WB_G1GetMixedGCInfo: G1 GC is not enabled"
); return __null; };
630 }
631 if (liveness < 0) {
632 THROW_MSG_NULL(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(), "liveness value should be non-negative"){ Exceptions::_throw_msg(__the_thread__, "/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 632, vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(), "liveness value should be non-negative"
); return __null; };
633 }
634
635 G1CollectedHeap* g1h = G1CollectedHeap::heap();
636 OldRegionsLivenessClosure rli(liveness);
637 g1h->heap_region_iterate(&rli);
638
639 typeArrayOop result = oopFactory::new_longArray(3, CHECK_NULL__the_thread__); if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) return __null; (void)(0);
640 result->long_at_put(0, rli.total_count());
641 result->long_at_put(1, rli.total_memory());
642 result->long_at_put(2, rli.total_memory_to_free());
643 return (jlongArray) JNIHandles::make_local(THREAD__the_thread__, result);
644WB_END} }

728static jmethodID reflected_method_to_jmid(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, jobject method) {
729 assert(method != NULL, "method should not be null")do { if (!(method != __null)) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error
("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 729, "assert(" "method != __null" ") failed", "method should not be null"
); ::breakpoint(); } } while (0);
730 ThreadToNativeFromVM ttn(thread);
731 return env->FromReflectedMethod(method);
732}
733
734// Deoptimizes all compiled frames and makes nmethods not entrant if it's requested
735class VM_WhiteBoxDeoptimizeFrames : public VM_WhiteBoxOperation {
736 private:
737 int _result;
738 const bool _make_not_entrant;
739 public:
740 VM_WhiteBoxDeoptimizeFrames(bool make_not_entrant) :
741 _result(0), _make_not_entrant(make_not_entrant) { }
742 int result() const { return _result; }
743
744 void doit() {
745 for (JavaThreadIteratorWithHandle jtiwh; JavaThread *t = jtiwh.next(); ) {
746 if (t->has_last_Java_frame()) {
747 for (StackFrameStream fst(t, false /* update */, true /* process_frames */); !fst.is_done(); fst.next()) {
748 frame* f = fst.current();
749 if (f->can_be_deoptimized() && !f->is_deoptimized_frame()) {
750 Deoptimization::deoptimize(t, *f);
751 if (_make_not_entrant) {
752 CompiledMethod* cm = CodeCache::find_compiled(f->pc());
753 assert(cm != NULL, "sanity check")do { if (!(cm != __null)) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error
("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 753, "assert(" "cm != __null" ") failed", "sanity check"); ::
breakpoint(); } } while (0);
754 cm->make_not_entrant();
755 }
756 ++_result;
757 }
758 }
759 }
760 }
761 }
762};
763
764WB_ENTRY(jint, WB_DeoptimizeFrames(JNIEnv* env, jobject o, jboolean make_not_entrant))extern "C" { jint WB_DeoptimizeFrames(JNIEnv* env, jobject o,
jboolean make_not_entrant) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::
thread_from_jni_environment(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread
|| (thread == Thread::current()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X'
;; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 764, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
765 VM_WhiteBoxDeoptimizeFrames op(make_not_entrant == JNI_TRUE1);
766 VMThread::execute(&op);
767 return op.result();
768WB_END} }

770WB_ENTRY(jboolean, WB_IsFrameDeoptimized(JNIEnv* env, jobject o, jint depth))extern "C" { jboolean WB_IsFrameDeoptimized(JNIEnv* env, jobject
o, jint depth) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current
()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"

") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;

788WB_ENTRY(jint, WB_DeoptimizeMethod(JNIEnv* env, jobject o, jobject method, jboolean is_osr))extern "C" { jint WB_DeoptimizeMethod(JNIEnv* env, jobject o,
jobject method, jboolean is_osr) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread
::thread_from_jni_environment(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread
|| (thread == Thread::current()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X'
;; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 788, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
789 jmethodID jmid = reflected_method_to_jmid(thread, env, method);
790 int result = 0;
791 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, result)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception

802 Deoptimization::deoptimize_all_marked();

818
819static bool is_excluded_for_compiler(AbstractCompiler* comp, methodHandle& mh) {
820 if (comp == NULL__null) {
821 return true;
822 }
823 DirectiveSet* directive = DirectivesStack::getMatchingDirective(mh, comp);
824 if (directive->ExcludeOption) {
825 return true;
826 }
827 return false;
828}
829
830static bool can_be_compiled_at_level(methodHandle& mh, jboolean is_osr, int level) {
831 if (is_osr) {
832 return CompilationPolicy::can_be_osr_compiled(mh, level);
833 } else {
834 return CompilationPolicy::can_be_compiled(mh, level);
835 }
836}
837
838WB_ENTRY(jboolean, WB_IsMethodCompilable(JNIEnv* env, jobject o, jobject method, jint comp_level, jboolean is_osr))extern "C" { jboolean WB_IsMethodCompilable(JNIEnv* env, jobject
o, jobject method, jint comp_level, jboolean is_osr) { JavaThread
* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment(env); do { if
(!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current()))) { (
*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 838, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
839 if (method == NULL__null || comp_level > CompilationPolicy::highest_compile_level()) {
840 return false;
841 }
842 jmethodID jmid = reflected_method_to_jmid(thread, env, method);
843 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, JNI_FALSE)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return(0); } } while (0);
844 MutexLocker mu(Compile_lock);
845 methodHandle mh(THREAD__the_thread__, Method::checked_resolve_jmethod_id(jmid));
846
847 // The ExcludeOption directive is evaluated lazily upon compilation attempt. If a method was not tried to be compiled by
848 // a compiler, yet, the method object is not set to be not compilable by that compiler. Thus, evaluate the compiler directive
849 // to exclude a compilation of 'method'.
850 if (comp_level == CompLevel_any) {
851 // Both compilers could have ExcludeOption set. Check all combinations.
852 bool excluded_c1 = is_excluded_for_compiler(CompileBroker::compiler1(), mh);
853 bool excluded_c2 = is_excluded_for_compiler(CompileBroker::compiler2(), mh);
854 if (excluded_c1 && excluded_c2) {
855 // Compilation of 'method' excluded by both compilers.
856 return false;
857 }
858
859 if (excluded_c1) {
860 // C1 only has ExcludeOption set: Check if compilable with C2.
861 return can_be_compiled_at_level(mh, is_osr, CompLevel_full_optimization);
862 } else if (excluded_c2) {
863 // C2 only has ExcludeOption set: Check if compilable with C1.
864 return can_be_compiled_at_level(mh, is_osr, CompLevel_simple);
865 }
866 } else if (comp_level > CompLevel_none && is_excluded_for_compiler(CompileBroker::compiler((int)comp_level), mh)) {
867 // Compilation of 'method' excluded by compiler used for 'comp_level'.
868 return false;
869 }

944WB_ENTRY(jint, WB_GetMethodTrapCount(JNIEnv* env, jobject o, jobject method, jstring reason_obj))extern "C" { jint WB_GetMethodTrapCount(JNIEnv* env, jobject o
, jobject method, jstring reason_obj) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread
::thread_from_jni_environment(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread
|| (thread == Thread::current()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X'
;; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 944, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
945 jmethodID jmid = reflected_method_to_jmid(thread, env, method);
946 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, 0)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return(0); } } while (0);
947 methodHandle mh(THREAD__the_thread__, Method::checked_resolve_jmethod_id(jmid));
948 uint cnt = 0;
949 MethodData* mdo = mh->method_data();
950 if (mdo != NULL__null) {
951 ResourceMark rm(THREAD__the_thread__);
952 char* reason_str = (reason_obj == NULL__null) ?
953 NULL__null : java_lang_String::as_utf8_string(JNIHandles::resolve_non_null(reason_obj));
954 bool overflow = false;
955 for (uint reason = 0; reason < mdo->trap_reason_limit(); reason++) {
956 if (reason_str != NULL__null && !strcmp(reason_str, Deoptimization::trap_reason_name(reason))) {
957 cnt = mdo->trap_count(reason);
958 // Count in the overflow trap count on overflow
959 if (cnt == (uint)-1) {
960 cnt = mdo->trap_count_limit() + mdo->overflow_trap_count();
961 }
962 break;
963 } else if (reason_str == NULL__null) {
964 uint c = mdo->trap_count(reason);
965 if (c == (uint)-1) {
966 c = mdo->trap_count_limit();
967 if (!overflow) {
968 // Count overflow trap count just once
969 overflow = true;
970 c += mdo->overflow_trap_count();
971 }
972 }
973 cnt += c;
974 }
975 }
976 }
977 return cnt;
978WB_END} }

1039
1040bool WhiteBox::compile_method(Method* method, int comp_level, int bci, JavaThread* THREAD__the_thread__) {
1041 // Screen for unavailable/bad comp level or null method
1042 AbstractCompiler* comp = CompileBroker::compiler(comp_level);
1043 if (method == NULL__null) {
1044 tty->print_cr("WB error: request to compile NULL method");
1045 return false;
1046 }
1047 if (comp_level > CompilationPolicy::highest_compile_level()) {
1048 tty->print_cr("WB error: invalid compilation level %d", comp_level);
1049 return false;
1050 }
1051 if (comp == NULL__null) {
1052 tty->print_cr("WB error: no compiler for requested compilation level %d", comp_level);
1053 return false;
1054 }
1055
1056 // Check if compilation is blocking
1057 methodHandle mh(THREAD__the_thread__, method);
1058 DirectiveSet* directive = DirectivesStack::getMatchingDirective(mh, comp);
1059 bool is_blocking = !directive->BackgroundCompilationOption;
1060 DirectivesStack::release(directive);
1061
1062 // Compile method and check result
1063 nmethod* nm = CompileBroker::compile_method(mh, bci, comp_level, mh, mh->invocation_count(), CompileTask::Reason_Whitebox, CHECK_false__the_thread__); if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) return false; (void)(0);
1064 MutexLocker mu(THREAD__the_thread__, Compile_lock);
1065 bool is_queued = mh->queued_for_compilation();
1066 if ((!is_blocking && is_queued) || nm != NULL__null) {
1067 return true;
1068 }
1069 // Check code again because compilation may be finished before Compile_lock is acquired.
1070 if (bci == InvocationEntryBci) {
1071 CompiledMethod* code = mh->code();
1072 if (code != NULL__null && code->as_nmethod_or_null() != NULL__null) {
1073 return true;
1074 }
1075 } else if (mh->lookup_osr_nmethod_for(bci, comp_level, false) != NULL__null) {
1076 return true;
1077 }
1078 tty->print("WB error: failed to %s compile at level %d method ", is_blocking ? "blocking" : "", comp_level);
1079 mh->print_short_name(tty);
1080 tty->cr();
1081 if (is_blocking && is_queued) {
1082 tty->print_cr("WB error: blocking compilation is still in queue!");
1083 }
1084 return false;
1085}

1215template <typename T, int type_enum>
1216static bool GetVMFlag(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, jstring name, T* value) {
1217 if (name == NULL__null) {
1218 return false;
1219 }
1220 ThreadToNativeFromVM ttnfv(thread); // can't be in VM when we call JNI
1221 const char* flag_name = env->GetStringUTFChars(name, NULL__null);
1222 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, false)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return(false); } } while (0);
1223 const JVMFlag* flag = JVMFlag::find_declared_flag(flag_name);
1224 JVMFlag::Error result = JVMFlagAccess::get<T, type_enum>(flag, value);
1225 env->ReleaseStringUTFChars(name, flag_name);
1226 return (result == JVMFlag::SUCCESS);
1227}
1228
1229template <typename T, int type_enum>
1230static bool SetVMFlag(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, jstring name, T* value) {
1231 if (name == NULL__null) {
1232 return false;
1233 }
1234 ThreadToNativeFromVM ttnfv(thread); // can't be in VM when we call JNI
1235 const char* flag_name = env->GetStringUTFChars(name, NULL__null);
1236 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, false)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return(false); } } while (0);
1237 JVMFlag* flag = JVMFlag::find_flag(flag_name);
1238 JVMFlag::Error result = JVMFlagAccess::set<T, type_enum>(flag, value, JVMFlagOrigin::INTERNAL);
1239 env->ReleaseStringUTFChars(name, flag_name);
1240 return (result == JVMFlag::SUCCESS);
1241}
1242
1243template <typename T>
1244static jobject box(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, Symbol* name, Symbol* sig, T value) {
1245 ResourceMark rm(thread);
1246 jclass clazz = env->FindClass(name->as_C_string());
1247 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, NULL)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return(__null); } } while (0);
1248 jmethodID methodID = env->GetStaticMethodID(clazz,
1249 vmSymbols::valueOf_name()->as_C_string(),
1250 sig->as_C_string());
1251 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, NULL)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return(__null); } } while (0);
1252 jobject result = env->CallStaticObjectMethod(clazz, methodID, value);
1253 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, NULL)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return(__null); } } while (0);
1254 return result;
1255}
1256
1257static jobject booleanBox(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, jboolean value) {
1258 return box(thread, env, vmSymbols::java_lang_Boolean(), vmSymbols::Boolean_valueOf_signature(), value);
1259}
1260static jobject integerBox(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, jint value) {
1261 return box(thread, env, vmSymbols::java_lang_Integer(), vmSymbols::Integer_valueOf_signature(), value);
1262}
1263static jobject longBox(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, jlong value) {
1264 return box(thread, env, vmSymbols::java_lang_Long(), vmSymbols::Long_valueOf_signature(), value);
1265}
1266/* static jobject floatBox(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, jfloat value) {
1267 return box(thread, env, vmSymbols::java_lang_Float(), vmSymbols::Float_valueOf_signature(), value);
1268}*/
1269static jobject doubleBox(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, jdouble value) {
1270 return box(thread, env, vmSymbols::java_lang_Double(), vmSymbols::Double_valueOf_signature(), value);
1271}

1454WB_ENTRY(void, WB_ReadReservedMemory(JNIEnv* env, jobject o))extern "C" { void WB_ReadReservedMemory(JNIEnv* env, jobject o
) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current
()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 1454, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
1455 // static+volatile in order to force the read to happen
1456 // (not be eliminated by the compiler)
1457 static char c;
1458 static volatile char* p;
1459
1460 p = os::reserve_memory(os::vm_allocation_granularity());
1461 if (p == NULL__null) {
1462 THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_OutOfMemoryError(), "Failed to reserve memory"){ Exceptions::_throw_msg(__the_thread__, "/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 1462, vmSymbols::java_lang_OutOfMemoryError(), "Failed to reserve memory"
); return; };
1463 }

1491 size(blob->size()),

1499};

1572CodeBlob* WhiteBox::allocate_code_blob(int size, int blob_type) {
1573 guarantee(WhiteBoxAPI, "internal testing API :: WhiteBox has to be enabled")do { if (!(WhiteBoxAPI)) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error
("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 1573, "guarantee(" "WhiteBoxAPI" ") failed", "internal testing API :: WhiteBox has to be enabled"
); ::breakpoint(); } } while (0);
1574 BufferBlob* blob;
1575 int full_size = CodeBlob::align_code_offset(sizeof(BufferBlob));
1576 if (full_size < size) {
1577 full_size += align_up(size - full_size, oopSize);
1578 }
1579 {
1580 MutexLocker mu(CodeCache_lock, Mutex::_no_safepoint_check_flag);
1581 blob = (BufferBlob*) CodeCache::allocate(full_size, blob_type);
1582 if (blob != NULL__null) {
1583 ::new (blob) BufferBlob("WB::DummyBlob", full_size);
1584 }
1585 }
1586 // Track memory usage statistic after releasing CodeCache_lock
1587 MemoryService::track_code_cache_memory_usage();
1588 return blob;
1589}

1851WB_ENTRY(jint, WB_ConstantPoolRemapInstructionOperandFromCache(JNIEnv* env, jobject wb, jclass klass, jint index))extern "C" { jint WB_ConstantPoolRemapInstructionOperandFromCache
(JNIEnv* env, jobject wb, jclass klass, jint index) { JavaThread
* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment(env); do { if
(!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current()))) { (
*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 1851, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
1852 InstanceKlass* ik = InstanceKlass::cast(java_lang_Class::as_Klass(JNIHandles::resolve(klass)));
1853 ConstantPool* cp = ik->constants();
1854 if (cp->cache() == NULL__null) {
1855 THROW_MSG_0(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalStateException(), "Constant pool does not have a cache"){ Exceptions::_throw_msg(__the_thread__, "/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"

); return 0; };
1856 }
1857 jint cpci = index;

1860 THROW_MSG_0(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(), "Constant pool cache index is out of range"){ Exceptions::_throw_msg(__the_thread__, "/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"

1875template <typename T>
1876static bool GetMethodOption(JavaThread* thread, JNIEnv* env, jobject method, jstring name, T* value) {
1877 assert(value != NULL, "sanity")do { if (!(value != __null)) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error
("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 1877, "assert(" "value != __null" ") failed", "sanity"); ::
breakpoint(); } } while (0);
1878 if (method == NULL__null || name == NULL__null) {
1879 return false;
1880 }
1881 jmethodID jmid = reflected_method_to_jmid(thread, env, method);
1882 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, false)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return(false); } } while (0);
1883 methodHandle mh(thread, Method::checked_resolve_jmethod_id(jmid));
1884 // can't be in VM when we call JNI
1885 ThreadToNativeFromVM ttnfv(thread);
1886 const char* flag_name = env->GetStringUTFChars(name, NULL__null);
1887 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION_(env, false)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return(false); } } while (0);
1888 enum CompileCommand option = CompilerOracle::string_to_option(flag_name);
1889 env->ReleaseStringUTFChars(name, flag_name);
1890 if (option == CompileCommand::Unknown) {
1891 return false;
1892 }
1893 if (!CompilerOracle::option_matches_type(option, *value)) {
1894 return false;
1895 }
1896 return CompilerOracle::has_option_value(mh, option, *value);
1897}

2070WB_ENTRY(jboolean, WB_HandshakeReadMonitors(JNIEnv* env, jobject wb, jobject thread_handle))extern "C" { jboolean WB_HandshakeReadMonitors(JNIEnv* env, jobject
wb, jobject thread_handle) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::
thread_from_jni_environment(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread
|| (thread == Thread::current()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X'
;; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 2070, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
2071 class ReadMonitorsClosure : public HandshakeClosure {
2072 jboolean _executed;
2073
2074 void do_thread(Thread* th) {
2075 JavaThread* jt = JavaThread::cast(th);
2076 ResourceMark rm;
2077
2078 GrowableArray<MonitorInfo*>* info = new GrowableArray<MonitorInfo*>();
2079
2080 if (!jt->has_last_Java_frame()) {
2081 return;
2082 }
2083 RegisterMap rmap(jt);
2084 for (javaVFrame* vf = jt->last_java_vframe(&rmap); vf != NULL__null; vf = vf->java_sender()) {
2085 GrowableArray<MonitorInfo*> *monitors = vf->monitors();
2086 if (monitors != NULL__null) {
2087 int len = monitors->length();
2088 // Walk monitors youngest to oldest
2089 for (int i = len - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
2090 MonitorInfo* mon_info = monitors->at(i);
2091 if (mon_info->eliminated()) continue;
2092 oop owner = mon_info->owner();
2093 if (owner != NULL__null) {
2094 info->append(mon_info);
2095 }
2096 }
2097 }
2098 }
2099 _executed = true;
2100 }
2101
2102 public:
2103 ReadMonitorsClosure() : HandshakeClosure("WB_HandshakeReadMonitors"), _executed(false) {}
2104 jboolean executed() const { return _executed; }
2105 };
2106
2107 ReadMonitorsClosure rmc;
2108 if (thread_handle != NULL__null) {
2109 ThreadsListHandle tlh;
2110 JavaThread* target = nullptr;
2111 bool is_alive = tlh.cv_internal_thread_to_JavaThread(thread_handle, &target, NULL__null);
2112 if (is_alive) {
2113 Handshake::execute(&rmc, &tlh, target);
2114 }
2115 }
2116 return rmc.executed();
2117WB_END} }

2182static volatile int _emulated_lock = 0;
2183
2184WB_ENTRY(void, WB_LockAndBlock(JNIEnv* env, jobject wb, jboolean suspender))extern "C" { void WB_LockAndBlock(JNIEnv* env, jobject wb, jboolean
suspender) { JavaThread* thread=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current
()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 2184, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
2185 JavaThread* self = JavaThread::current();
2186
2187 {
2188 // Before trying to acquire the lock transition into a safepoint safe state.
2189 // Otherwise if either suspender or suspendee blocks for a safepoint
2190 // in ~ThreadBlockInVM the other one could loop forever trying to acquire
2191 // the lock without allowing the safepoint to progress.
2192 ThreadBlockInVM tbivm(self);
2193
2194 // We will deadlock here if we are 'suspender' and 'suspendee'
2195 // suspended in ~ThreadBlockInVM. This verifies we only suspend
2196 // at the right place.
2197 while (Atomic::cmpxchg(&_emulated_lock, 0, 1) != 0) {}
2198 assert(_emulated_lock == 1, "Must be locked")do { if (!(_emulated_lock == 1)) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';;
report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 2198, "assert(" "_emulated_lock == 1" ") failed", "Must be locked"
); ::breakpoint(); } } while (0);
2199
2200 // Sleep much longer in suspendee to force situation where
2201 // 'suspender' is waiting above to acquire lock.
2202 os::naked_short_sleep(suspender ? 1 : 10);
2203 }
2204 Atomic::store(&_emulated_lock, 0);
2205WB_END} }
2206
2207// Some convenience methods to deal with objects from java
2208int WhiteBox::offset_for_field(const char* field_name, oop object,
2209 Symbol* signature_symbol) {
2210 assert(field_name != NULL && strlen(field_name) > 0, "Field name not valid")do { if (!(field_name != __null && strlen(field_name)
> 0)) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 2210, "assert(" "field_name != __null && strlen(field_name) > 0"
") failed", "Field name not valid"); ::breakpoint(); } } while
(0);
2211
2212 //Get the class of our object
2213 Klass* arg_klass = object->klass();
2214 //Turn it into an instance-klass
2215 InstanceKlass* ik = InstanceKlass::cast(arg_klass);
2216
2217 //Create symbols to look for in the class
2218 TempNewSymbol name_symbol = SymbolTable::new_symbol(field_name);
2219
2220 //To be filled in with an offset of the field we're looking for
2221 fieldDescriptor fd;
2222
2223 Klass* res = ik->find_field(name_symbol, signature_symbol, &fd);
2224 if (res == NULL__null) {
2225 tty->print_cr("Invalid layout of %s at %s", ik->external_name(),
2226 name_symbol->as_C_string());
2227 vm_exit_during_initialization("Invalid layout of preloaded class: use -Xlog:class+load=info to see the origin of the problem class");
2228 }
2229
2230 //fetch the field at the offset we've found
2231 int dest_offset = fd.offset();
2232
2233 return dest_offset;
2234}

2237const char* WhiteBox::lookup_jstring(const char* field_name, oop object) {
2238 int offset = offset_for_field(field_name, object,
2239 vmSymbols::string_signature());
2240 oop string = object->obj_field(offset);
2241 if (string == NULL__null) {
2242 return NULL__null;
2243 }
2244 const char* ret = java_lang_String::as_utf8_string(string);
2245 return ret;
2246}

2248bool WhiteBox::lookup_bool(const char* field_name, oop object) {
2249 int offset =
2250 offset_for_field(field_name, object, vmSymbols::bool_signature());
2251 bool ret = (object->bool_field(offset) == JNI_TRUE1);
2252 return ret;
2253}

2255void WhiteBox::register_methods(JNIEnv* env, jclass wbclass, JavaThread* thread, JNINativeMethod* method_array, int method_count) {
2256 ResourceMark rm;
2257 Klass* klass = java_lang_Class::as_Klass(JNIHandles::resolve_non_null(wbclass));
2258 const char* klass_name = klass->external_name();
2259
2260 ThreadToNativeFromVM ttnfv(thread); // can't be in VM when we call JNI
2261
2262 // one by one registration natives for exception catching
2263 jclass no_such_method_error_klass = env->FindClass(vmSymbols::java_lang_NoSuchMethodError()->as_C_string());
2264 CHECK_JNI_EXCEPTION(env)do { JavaThread* __the_thread__ = JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment
(env); __the_thread__->clear_pending_jni_exception_check()
; if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) { return; } } while (0);
2265 for (int i = 0, n = method_count; i < n; ++i) {
2266 // Skip dummy entries
2267 if (method_array[i].fnPtr == NULL__null) continue;
2268 if (env->RegisterNatives(wbclass, &method_array[i], 1) != 0) {
2269 jthrowable throwable_obj = env->ExceptionOccurred();
2270 if (throwable_obj != NULL__null) {
2271 env->ExceptionClear();
2272 if (env->IsInstanceOf(throwable_obj, no_such_method_error_klass)) {
2273 // NoSuchMethodError is thrown when a method can't be found or a method is not native.
2274 // Ignoring the exception since it is not preventing use of other WhiteBox methods.
2275 tty->print_cr("Warning: 'NoSuchMethodError' on register of %s::%s%s",
2276 klass_name, method_array[i].name, method_array[i].signature);
2277 }
2278 } else {
2279 // Registration failed unexpectedly.
2280 tty->print_cr("Warning: unexpected error on register of %s::%s%s. All methods will be unregistered",
2281 klass_name, method_array[i].name, method_array[i].signature);
2282 env->UnregisterNatives(wbclass);
2283 break;
2284 }
2285 }
2286 }
2287}

2380// See test/hotspot/jtreg/runtime/Thread/ThreadObjAccessAtExit.java.
2381// It explains how the thread's priority field is used for test state coordination.
2382//
2383WB_ENTRY(void, WB_CheckThreadObjOfTerminatingThread(JNIEnv* env, jobject wb, jobject target_handle))extern "C" { void WB_CheckThreadObjOfTerminatingThread(JNIEnv
* env, jobject wb, jobject target_handle) { JavaThread* thread
=JavaThread::thread_from_jni_environment(env); do { if (!(!VerifyJNIEnvThread
|| (thread == Thread::current()))) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X'
;; report_vm_error("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 2383, "assert(" "!VerifyJNIEnvThread || (thread == Thread::current())"
") failed", "JNIEnv is only valid in same thread"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0); ; ThreadInVMfromNative __tiv(thread); VMNativeEntryWrapper
__vew; HandleMarkCleaner __hm(thread); JavaThread* __the_thread__
= thread; os::verify_stack_alignment(); WeakPreserveExceptionMark
__wem(thread); ClearPendingJniExcCheck _clearCheck(env); ;
2384 oop target_oop = JNIHandles::resolve_non_null(target_handle);
2385 jlong tid = java_lang_Thread::thread_id(target_oop);
2386 JavaThread* target = java_lang_Thread::thread(target_oop);
2387
2388 // Grab a ThreadsListHandle to protect the target thread whilst terminating
2389 ThreadsListHandle tlh;
2390
2391 // Look up the target thread by tid to ensure it is present
2392 JavaThread* t = tlh.list()->find_JavaThread_from_java_tid(tid);
2393 if (t == NULL__null) {
2394 THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_RuntimeException(), "Target thread not found in ThreadsList!"){ Exceptions::_throw_msg(__the_thread__, "/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 2394, vmSymbols::java_lang_RuntimeException(), "Target thread not found in ThreadsList!"
); return; };
2395 }
2396
2397 tty->print_cr("WB_CheckThreadObjOfTerminatingThread: target thread is protected");
2398 // Allow target to terminate by boosting priority
2399 java_lang_Thread::set_priority(t->threadObj(), ThreadPriority(NormPriority + 1));
2400
2401 // Now wait for the target to terminate
2402 while (!target->is_terminated()) {
2403 ThreadBlockInVM tbivm(thread); // just in case target is involved in a safepoint
2404 os::naked_short_sleep(0);
2405 }
2406
2407 tty->print_cr("WB_CheckThreadObjOfTerminatingThread: target thread is terminated");
2408
2409 // Now release the GC inducing thread - we have to re-resolve the external oop that
2410 // was passed in as GC may have occurred and we don't know if we can trust t->threadObj() now.
2411 oop original = JNIHandles::resolve_non_null(target_handle);
2412 java_lang_Thread::set_priority(original, ThreadPriority(NormPriority + 2));
2413
2414 tty->print_cr("WB_CheckThreadObjOfTerminatingThread: GC has been initiated - checking threadObj:");
2415
2416 // The Java code should be creating garbage and triggering GC, which would potentially move
2417 // the threadObj oop. If the exiting thread is properly protected then its threadObj should
2418 // remain valid and equal to our initial target_handle. Loop a few times to give GC a chance to
2419 // kick in.
2420 for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
2421 oop original = JNIHandles::resolve_non_null(target_handle);
2422 oop current = t->threadObj();
2423 if (original != current) {
2424 tty->print_cr("WB_CheckThreadObjOfTerminatingThread: failed comparison on iteration %d", i);
2425 THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_RuntimeException(), "Target thread oop has changed!"){ Exceptions::_throw_msg(__the_thread__, "/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/prims/whitebox.cpp"
, 2425, vmSymbols::java_lang_RuntimeException(), "Target thread oop has changed!"
); return; };
2426 } else {
2427 tty->print_cr("WB_CheckThreadObjOfTerminatingThread: successful comparison on iteration %d", i);
2428 ThreadBlockInVM tbivm(thread);
2429 os::naked_short_sleep(50);
2430 }
2431 }

33// This file provides the basic support for exception handling in the VM.
34// Note: We do not use C++ exceptions to avoid compiler dependencies and
35// unpredictable performance.
36//
37// Scheme: Exceptions are stored with the thread. There is never more
38// than one pending exception per thread. All functions that can throw
39// an exception carry a THREAD argument (usually the last argument and
40// declared with the TRAPS macro). Throwing an exception means setting
41// a pending exception in the thread. Upon return from a function that
42// can throw an exception, we must check if an exception is pending.
43// The CHECK macros do this in a convenient way. Carrying around the
44// thread provides also convenient access to it (e.g. for Handle
45// creation, w/o the need for recomputation).
46
47
48
49// Forward declarations to be independent of the include structure.
50
51class JavaThread;
52class Handle;
53class Symbol;
54class JavaCallArguments;
55class methodHandle;
56
57// The ThreadShadow class is a helper class to access the _pending_exception
58// field of the Thread class w/o having access to the Thread's interface (for
59// include hierachy reasons).
60
61class ThreadShadow: public CHeapObj<mtThread> {
62 friend class VMStructs;
63 friend class JVMCIVMStructs;
64
65 protected:
66 oop _pending_exception; // Thread has gc actions.
67 const char* _exception_file; // file information for exception (debugging only)
68 int _exception_line; // line information for exception (debugging only)
69 friend void check_ThreadShadow(); // checks _pending_exception offset
70
71 // The following virtual exists only to force creation of a vtable.
72 // We need ThreadShadow to have a vtable, even in product builds,
73 // so that its layout will start at an offset of zero relative to Thread.
74 // Some C++ compilers are so "clever" that they put the ThreadShadow
75 // base class at offset 4 in Thread (after Thread's vtable), if they
76 // notice that Thread has a vtable but ThreadShadow does not.
77 virtual void unused_initial_virtual() { }
78
79 public:
80 oop pending_exception() const { return _pending_exception; }
81 bool has_pending_exception() const { return _pending_exception != NULL__null; }
8
←
Calling 'oop::operator!='
→
11
←
Returning from 'oop::operator!='
→
12
←
Returning zero, which participates in a condition later
→
82 const char* exception_file() const { return _exception_file; }
83 int exception_line() const { return _exception_line; }
84
85 // Code generation support
86 static ByteSize pending_exception_offset() { return byte_offset_of(ThreadShadow, _pending_exception)in_ByteSize((int)(size_t)((intx)&(((ThreadShadow*)16)->
_pending_exception) - 16)); }
87
88 // use THROW whenever possible!
89 void set_pending_exception(oop exception, const char* file, int line);
90
91 // use CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION whenever possible!
92 void clear_pending_exception();
93
94 // use CLEAR_PENDING_NONASYNC_EXCEPTION to clear probable nonasync exception.
95 void clear_pending_nonasync_exception();
96
97 ThreadShadow() : _pending_exception(NULL__null),
98 _exception_file(NULL__null), _exception_line(0) {}
99};

198// The THREAD & TRAPS macros facilitate the declaration of functions that throw exceptions.
199// Convention: Use the TRAPS macro as the last argument of such a function; e.g.:
200//
201// int this_function_may_trap(int x, float y, TRAPS)
202
203#define THREAD__the_thread__ __the_thread__
204#define TRAPSJavaThread* __the_thread__ JavaThread* THREAD__the_thread__
205
206
207// The CHECK... macros should be used to pass along a THREAD reference and to check for pending
208// exceptions. In special situations it is necessary to handle pending exceptions explicitly,
209// in these cases the PENDING_EXCEPTION helper macros should be used.
210//
211// Macro naming conventions: Macros that end with _ require a result value to be returned. They
212// are for functions with non-void result type. The result value is usually ignored because of
213// the exception and is only needed for syntactic correctness. The _0 ending is a shortcut for
214// _(0) since this is a frequent case. Example:
215//
216// int result = this_function_may_trap(x_arg, y_arg, CHECK_0);
217//
218// CAUTION: make sure that the function call using a CHECK macro is not the only statement of a
219// conditional branch w/o enclosing {} braces, since the CHECK macros expand into several state-
220// ments! Also make sure it is not used on a function call that is part of a return statement!
221
222#define PENDING_EXCEPTION(((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->pending_exception()) (((ThreadShadow*)THREAD__the_thread__)->pending_exception())
223#define HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION(((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception()) (((ThreadShadow*)THREAD__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception())
224#define CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION(((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->clear_pending_exception(
)) (((ThreadShadow*)THREAD__the_thread__)->clear_pending_exception())
225

())) return ; (void)(0 THREAD__the_thread__); if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION(((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception())) return ; (void)(0
227#define CHECK_(result)__the_thread__); if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) return result; (void)(0 THREAD__the_thread__); if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION(((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception())) return result; (void)(0
228#define CHECK_0__the_thread__); if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) return 0; (void)(0 CHECK_(0)__the_thread__); if ((((ThreadShadow*)__the_thread__)->has_pending_exception
())) return 0; (void)(0

32// OBJECT hierarchy
33// This hierarchy is a representation hierarchy, i.e. if A is a superclass
34// of B, A's representation is a prefix of B's representation.
35
36// Global offset instead of address for an oop within a java object.
37enum class narrowOop : uint32_t { null = 0 };

39// If compressed klass pointers then use narrowKlass.

44#ifndef CHECK_UNHANDLED_OOPS1
45
46typedef class oopDesc* oop;
47typedef class instanceOopDesc* instanceOop;
48typedef class arrayOopDesc* arrayOop;
49typedef class objArrayOopDesc* objArrayOop;
50typedef class typeArrayOopDesc* typeArrayOop;
51
52#else
53
54// When CHECK_UNHANDLED_OOPS is defined, an "oop" is a class with a
55// carefully chosen set of constructors and conversion operators to go
56// to and from the underlying oopDesc pointer type.
57//
58// Because oop and its subclasses <type>Oop are class types, arbitrary
59// conversions are not accepted by the compiler. Applying a cast to
60// an oop will cause the best matched conversion operator to be
61// invoked returning the underlying oopDesc* type if appropriate.
62// No copy constructors, explicit user conversions or operators of
63// numerical type should be defined within the oop class. Most C++
64// compilers will issue a compile time error concerning the overloading
65// ambiguity between operators of numerical and pointer types. If
66// a conversion to or from an oop to a numerical type is needed,
67// use the inline template methods, cast_*_oop, defined below.
68//
69// Converting NULL to oop to Handle implicit is no longer accepted by the
70// compiler because there are too many steps in the conversion. Use Handle()
71// instead, which generates less code anyway.
72
73class Thread;
74class oopDesc;
75
76extern "C" bool CheckUnhandledOops;
77
78class oop {
79 oopDesc* _o;
80
81 void register_oop();
82 void unregister_oop();
83
84 void register_if_checking() {
85 if (CheckUnhandledOops) register_oop();
86 }
87
88public:
89 oop() : _o(nullptr) { register_if_checking(); }
90 oop(const oop& o) : _o(o._o) { register_if_checking(); }
91 oop(oopDesc* o) : _o(o) { register_if_checking(); }
92 ~oop() {
93 if (CheckUnhandledOops) unregister_oop();
94 }
95
96 oopDesc* obj() const { return _o; }
97 oopDesc* operator->() const { return _o; }
98 operator oopDesc* () const { return _o; }
99
100 bool operator==(const oop& o) const { return _o == o._o; }
101 bool operator!=(const oop& o) const { return _o != o._o; }
102
103 bool operator==(std::nullptr_t) const { return _o == nullptr; }
104 bool operator!=(std::nullptr_t) const { return _o != nullptr; }
9
←
Assuming the condition is false
→
10
←
Returning zero, which participates in a condition later
→
105
106 oop& operator=(const oop& o) { _o = o._o; return *this; }
107};
108
109template<>
110struct PrimitiveConversions::Translate<oop> : public TrueType {
111 typedef oop Value;
112 typedef oopDesc* Decayed;
113
114 static Decayed decay(Value x) { return x.obj(); }
115 static Value recover(Decayed x) { return oop(x); }
116};

43// CompilerCounters
44//
45// Per Compiler Performance Counters.
46//
47class CompilerCounters : public CHeapObj<mtCompiler> {
48
49 public:
50 enum {
51 cmname_buffer_length = 160
52 };
53
54 private:
55
56 char _current_method[cmname_buffer_length];
57 int _compile_type;
58
59 public:
60 CompilerCounters();
61
62 // these methods should be called in a thread safe context
63
64 void set_current_method(const char* method) {
65 strncpy(_current_method, method, (size_t)cmname_buffer_length-1);
66 _current_method[cmname_buffer_length-1] = '\0';
67 }
68
69 char* current_method() { return _current_method; }
70
71 void set_compile_type(int compile_type) {
72 _compile_type = compile_type;
73 }
74
75 int compile_type() { return _compile_type; }
76
77};

79// CompileQueue

83 private:

86 CompileTask* _first;
87 CompileTask* _last;
88
89 CompileTask* _first_stale;
90
91 int _size;
92
93 void purge_stale_tasks();
94 public:
95 CompileQueue(const char* name) {
96 _name = name;
97 _first = NULL__null;
98 _last = NULL__null;
99 _size = 0;
100 _first_stale = NULL__null;
101 }
102
103 const char* name() const { return _name; }
104
105 void add(CompileTask* task);
106 void remove(CompileTask* task);
107 void remove_and_mark_stale(CompileTask* task);
108 CompileTask* first() { return _first; }
109 CompileTask* last() { return _last; }
110
111 CompileTask* get();
112
113 bool is_empty() const { return _first == NULL__null; }
114 int size() const { return _size; }
115
116
117 // Redefine Classes support
118 void mark_on_stack();
119 void free_all();
120 void print_tty();
121 void print(outputStream* st = tty);
122
123 ~CompileQueue() {
124 assert (is_empty(), " Compile Queue must be empty")do { if (!(is_empty())) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error
("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/compiler/compileBroker.hpp"
, 124, "assert(" "is_empty()" ") failed", " Compile Queue must be empty"
); ::breakpoint(); } } while (0);
125 }
126};

128// CompileTaskWrapper
129//

131// when the compilation is complete.

135 ~CompileTaskWrapper();
136};

283 static AbstractCompiler* compiler(int comp_level) {
284 if (is_c2_compile(comp_level)) return _compilers[1]; // C2
17
←
Taking true branch
→
18
←
Returning pointer
→
285 if (is_c1_compile(comp_level)) return _compilers[0]; // C1
286 return NULL__null;
287 }

329 enum CompilerActivity {
330 // Flags for toggling compiler activity
331 stop_compilation = 0,
332 run_compilation = 1,
333 shutdown_compilation = 2
334 };
335
336 static jint get_compilation_activity_mode() { return _should_compile_new_jobs; }
337 static bool should_compile_new_jobs() { return UseCompiler && (_should_compile_new_jobs == run_compilation); }
338 static bool set_should_compile_new_jobs(jint new_state) {
339 // Return success if the current caller set it
340 jint old = Atomic::cmpxchg(&_should_compile_new_jobs, 1-new_state, new_state);
341 bool success = (old == (1-new_state));
342 if (success) {
343 if (new_state == run_compilation) {
344 _total_compiler_restarted_count++;
345 } else {
346 _total_compiler_stopped_count++;
347 }
348 }
349 return success;
350 }
351
352 static void disable_compilation_forever() {
353 UseCompiler = false;
354 AlwaysCompileLoopMethods = false;
355 Atomic::xchg(&_should_compile_new_jobs, jint(shutdown_compilation));
356 }
357
358 static bool is_compilation_disabled_forever() {
359 return _should_compile_new_jobs == shutdown_compilation;
360 }
361 static void handle_full_code_cache(int code_blob_type);
362 // Ensures that warning is only printed once.
363 static bool should_print_compiler_warning() {
364 jint old = Atomic::cmpxchg(&_print_compilation_warning, 0, 1);
365 return old == 0;
366 }
367 // Return total compilation ticks
368 static jlong total_compilation_ticks();

, 384, "assert(" "_compiler1_objects != __null" ") failed", "must be initialized"
); ::breakpoint(); } } while (0);
385 assert(idx < _c1_count, "oob")do { if (!(idx < _c1_count)) { (*g_assert_poison) = 'X';; report_vm_error
("/home/daniel/Projects/java/jdk/src/hotspot/share/compiler/compileBroker.hpp"
, 385, "assert(" "idx < _c1_count" ") failed", "oob"); ::breakpoint
(); } } while (0);

387 }
